This reformulation is simpler to derive, produces straighter trajectories (fewer function evaluations at inference), and generalizes naturally to any source-target pair rather than requiring a Gaussian source. Consistency models (Song et al., 2023) take a further step: instead of learning a multi-step process, they learn a function that maps any point on a diffusion trajectory directly to the clean sample in a single evaluation. Together, these methods represent the frontier of fast generative inference."}],"\n",["$","hr",null,{"style":{"border":"none","borderTop":"1px solid var(--border-subtle)","margin":"2.5em
